British Defense Mega-Plan Emphasizes Strengthening the Air Force, Aiming to Complete Within Ten Years; Seeks Close Liaison with Territories; Unwilling to Lag Behind in the Arms Race 29

(London) Following yesterday's cabinet meeting, according to sources in diplomatic circles today, Britain's plan to expand its air force is about to mature rapidly. The rumor that the government will submit a huge supplementary budget for the air force to Parliament next week, which was circulated yesterday morning, has been denied by reliable sources this morning. However, it is indeed expected that a supplementary budget will be submitted before the House adjourns next month. According to well-informed sources, the air force expansion plan will increase the budget by a much higher amount than that proposed by the army and navy. It has long been rumored that the British government intends to double the air force strength of the army and navy within five years. Today, this seems to be confirmed. However, some parties say that the expansion period is seven or ten years rather than five years. However, it is already obvious that this expansion plan has matured. The government and influential newspapers such as the Daily Mail, the Daily Express, and the Evening Standard have all made the public understand the necessity of air defense preparations, and the whole country must work together to contribute to promoting this move. According to experts, if Britain doubles its air force, including flight personnel and airports, it will cost 25 million pounds. Therefore, the government has decided to implement it with a long-term plan. If the government completes this move within one year, it must increase taxes. This kind of adventurous move is not dare to be done by the current cabinet, and government officials also believe that there is no danger of war at present, so it is okay to proceed gradually, so that the British air force, which is currently ranked sixth in the world, gradually becomes equal to the air force strength of other European countries. Generally, Britain may first slightly reveal its intention to expand, so that France and Germany can see that the air force competition will tend to extremes, or may finally comply with Britain's intention and establish a treaty restricting international air forces. This treaty is now opposed by France. The Disarmament Conference has repeatedly been on the verge of collapse, and the air force agreement proposed by Britain is the last effort to save it. If it cannot succeed, Britain will expand its existing 1,500 aircraft to 3,000 aircraft to be equal to France. The plan announced by the government is that the British air force must be equal to the country with the strongest air force within striking distance. Everyone knows that the German air force can already compete with France, and it is rumored that it is still expanding secretly, so Britain has to catch up urgently. As for the United States, Britain feels even more inferior when compared with it. This is also an important reason why those who advocate expanding the air force see it. (National News Agency dispatch from the 27th)

(London) British Secretary of State for Air Londonderry stated in the House of Lords today the British government's resolution to have an air force equal to that of other countries in the world in a short period of time. His statement was roughly the same as that made by Lord Privy Seal Baldwin recently. The Secretary of State for Air's remarks were in response to a question from Lord Mottistone, who said that British air defenses were weak and should be remedied. The Secretary of State for Air replied that it was almost hopeless to obtain an international convention to solve this problem in Europe, so the British government decided not to delay any longer and immediately take the necessary steps to make British air defenses perfect. As for the details of how the air force will be expanded, it is not convenient to publish them at present, but there is no need to worry. The plan and methods for expanding the air force are now fully underway. The Secretary of State for Air also answered a question from Lord Elibank, saying that the self-governing territories and the British government both feel that the plan to establish a centralized air force in the British Empire is not in line with the autonomy of all parties, but they are now trying to make the air forces in all parts of the British Empire closely linked within the possible scope. (Reuters dispatch from the 27th)

US Seems to Tacitly Approve of British Military Expansion Request 30

(Washington) The unofficial reaction here to the British shipbuilding program is growing, and everyone thinks that the program is a legitimate action. However, those who hope that next year's conference can obtain a real naval disarmament result are inevitably disappointed. The naval expansion program in London seems unreasonable at first glance, but it seems otherwise due to the following factors: The collapse of the Geneva Disarmament Conference, the ship-increasing program of Italy and France, and Japan's request for equality all make Britain deeply believe in the importance of prevention and are eager to consolidate its naval position. Some people think that the British program is actually running parallel to the US shipbuilding program. Now the US has decided to expand its navy to the extent permitted by the treaty, and has approved the construction of as many as 50 warships. Some people think that the British program, at least in part, is to consolidate its position at the opening of next year's naval conference, so that it can have something to rely on when negotiating. (National News Agency dispatch from the 27th)

Disarmament Committee Continues its Work; Study Group on Cracking Down on Arms Manufacturing Meets; Chairman Proposes Draft Advocating Adoption of Supervisory System 40

(Geneva) On the 11th of this month, the General Committee of the Disarmament Conference established four committees in accordance with the compromise plan proposed by Barthou to study separately: 1. Security, 2. Supervision, 3. Aviation, 4. Arms Manufacturing and Trafficking. Recently, the first, second, and fourth committees have all met. Today, the subcommittee specializing in the study of arms manufacturing problems of the fourth committee held another meeting. The chairman, the Polish representative, presented a draft to the subcommittee, which only stipulated universal crackdown measures on arms manufacturing, but advocated that both state-owned and private manufacturing should be cracked down on equally. The draft, on the one hand, advocated the adoption of a comprehensive supervisory system domestically, and on the other hand, set up supervisory methods internationally, but what was proposed was only a supervision outline, and the detailed methods will be discussed later. Today, the proposer, the Polish representative, explained the reason, saying that according to the new principle, all countries should bear responsibilities within the scope of the international disarmament convention, and the draft he proposed is a practical way to implement this new principle. War Debt Issue; Britain Replies to the US Again; Opposes Paying Debt with Goods 42

(Washington) British Ambassador to the United States, Lindsay, has today sent the British government's reply to the US Secretary of State Hull regarding the repayment of debt with goods. The reply stated that the experience of Germany repaying debt with goods has shown that replacing cash with goods still cannot avoid the difficulty of unlocking funds. The United Kingdom believes that after the repayment of debt with goods, the US exports to the United Kingdom will be greatly damaged, and if the goods sold by the United Kingdom in the United States cannot recover cash, then the United Kingdom's ability to purchase US cotton and other goods will be further reduced. Therefore, although the British government is willing to continue discussing the debt issue, it feels that the plan proposed by the United States is not feasible. The reply continued that the difficulty of repaying debt with goods is equal to that of repaying debt with cash, unless these goods are produced in the debtor country and the creditor country accepts them in addition to the original import. As for the final section of the reply, the United Kingdom expressed in a friendly tone that the crux of the war debt issue lies in the number. The reply said, "In view of the various circumstances related to this debt, the British government is very willing to re-discuss it after the current abnormal state is improved, so that a solution can be obtained, because the United Kingdom is also eager to remove the source of the dispute as soon as possible, so as not to hinder harmonious relations." (National News Agency dispatch from the 27th)

Anglo-French Trade Agreement Concluded; Retaliatory Tariffs Declared Abolished 43

(London) The Anglo-French trade war will end on Sunday, and if the negotiations between Britain and Germany are not smooth, the two countries will start a trade war on that day. Representatives of Britain and France signed an agreement here today to end the commercial dispute between the two countries. The agreement will take effect from Sunday. The two countries will cancel the allocation and retaliatory tariffs. Before June 10, the treaty was in draft. On June 10, it was announced that the trade agreement had been concluded. The two countries abolished retaliatory measures and mutually granted the most-favored-nation tariff and other commercial terms to each other. (National News Agency dispatch from the 27th)

(London) The Anglo-French trade agreement was officially signed at 5 pm. The following is a record of the negotiations between the two countries: Since the devaluation of the British pound, France, in order to prevent the dumping of British goods, imposed an exchange rate adjustment surcharge of 15% on British goods and restricted the quantity of British goods imported. Although this tariff rate was cancelled from January 1st of this year, France reduced the quota for British goods imported by 75%. The United Kingdom's negotiations were ineffective, so in February, it imposed an additional tariff of 21% on certain French goods in retaliation. As a result, France also announced the abolition of the Anglo-French Treaty of Commerce and Navigation of 1882. Later, the governments of the two countries, in view of the fact that mutual retaliation was not a good strategy, held trade negotiations in March. The negotiations were once interrupted, but they restarted at the beginning of this month. The negotiations were concluded on the 16th, and the trade agreement was initialed on that day. (Havas dispatch from the 27th)

U.S. Government Purchases Silver, Arousing Attention from All Sides 44

(Washington) The U.S. government's decision to begin purchasing large quantities of silver, absorbing 135.4 million ounces within six months, has attracted attention everywhere. However, Treasury Department officials are unwilling to discuss the silver issue. Although the Treasury Department currently has the authority to purchase over 100 million ounces of silver, whether it will purchase such a large amount had not been definitively decided as of last month. Treasury Department officials are unwilling to comment on Representative Dies' statement yesterday that the Treasury Department has already purchased 75 million ounces of silver. In short, the Treasury Department is unwilling to disclose the amount of silver it has purchased. It is understood that the funds for purchasing the silver are mostly allocated from the Exchange Equalization Fund, so the quantity is not recorded in the Treasury Department's daily report. The Treasury Department now plans to purchase silver from ordinary expenses in the future. If so, the amount of silver purchased will be visible in the central government's daily reports. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(Washington) The U.S. Internal Revenue Commissioner today ordered silver brokers who purchase long positions on behalf of foreign clients to immediately ask their clients to swear and complete a statement of facts. This is because, according to U.S. law, if these long positions are closed after September 1st, a statement must be submitted upon closing. If a client statement is not obtained by then, the broker must complete it on behalf of the client when the long position is closed. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

Commemoration of the Treaty of Versailles: Germans Do Not Forget the Humiliating Treaty; National Half-Mast Flags Mark National Shame; Berliners' Hearts Are Exceptionally Agitated 46

(Berlin) Today is the 15th anniversary of the signing of the Treaty of Versailles. All German public and private institutions are flying flags at half-mast to mark the shame. This is not only a clear expression of the German government's aversion to the Treaty of Versailles, but also a symbol of the painful feelings of the German people. Some morning newspapers used black borders, reminding people of the humiliating and miserable scene when Germany was forced to sign the treaty fifteen years ago. It is said that the treaty not only failed to bring peace to Europe and the world, but instead brought the opposite disaster. (National News Agency dispatch, 28th)

(Berlin) Today is the 15th anniversary of the signing of the Treaty of Versailles, and also the 20th anniversary of the Sarajevo Incident (a place name, formerly part of the Austrian province of Bosnia, now ceded to Yugoslavia. On June 28, 1914, a Serbian student, Princip, assassinated the Austrian Archduke Franz Ferdinand and his wife in that location, triggering the outbreak of the European War). The newspapers in the German capital have written extensively about it, especially expressing dissatisfaction with the so-called "humiliating treaty" of Versailles, stating that the Treaty of Versailles is not another name for peace, and fiercely criticizing the Allied countries, especially France. The Berlin Stock Exchange News stated that the Treaty of Versailles was a fraudulent act of coercion during Germany's exhaustion and should not be regarded as a treaty. The Berlin Morning News asked, "Today, the whole country

flies flags at half-mast, to protest the Allied countries' use of violence and coercion, and as a symbol of the struggle for honorable peace and equal rights." In addition, the German Public Organizations Joint Committee issued a declaration opposing Germany's current borders, stating that they are "contrary to common sense." The association also expressed resistance to the various countries' deprivation of German colonies, stating that this kind of deprivation action "reduces the land crucial to the survival of the German nation," which is intolerable. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Renowned British Reporter Reveals German Military Secrets: Prepared to Release Poison Gas Once the European War Breaks Out 47

(London) The July issue of "The Nineteenth Century" magazine publishes an article by renowned British author Wickham Steed (former editor-in-chief of The Times), revealing the secret of Germany's preparation of poison gas, which is profound and moving. Hitler Asks a Blind Fortune Teller, Who Tells Him He Can Still Govern for Thirty Years, Followed by Hindenburg, Who Will Be Over Seventy Years Old 48

(Berlin) Recently, there have been many speculations about Prime Minister Hitler and Propaganda Minister Goebbels. Now, I will record two things for your amusement. One day, Hitler visited an astrologer to ask about his fortune. Hitler asked how many years he could still rule Germany. The astrologer told him that there were still thirty years. Hitler replied that it was good, but then who would succeed him? The astrologer replied with Hindenburg. President Hindenburg is already eighty-seven years old and has been in charge of the central government for many years. The Germans worship him like a god. Whether the astrologer's words are credible is debatable. However, in today's Germany, except for those with scientific basis, all astrologers have been banned. This is one thing. People in Berlin can all talk about it. There is also one thing about Propaganda Minister Goebbels. Since Vice Prime Minister von Papen made a sharp criticism of the Nazi Party's maladministration, Propaganda Minister Goebbels has been carrying out a purge of newspapers across the country. Ministry of Finance Bribery Case Report Completed: Japanese Political Situation Tense Again: Saitō Visits Takahashi 56

(Tokyo) The interim report on the Ministry of Finance case is imminent, so the attitudes of the Prime Minister and the Finance Minister are attracting great public attention. Today, Prime Minister Saitō suddenly visited Finance Minister Takahashi at his official residence in Nagatachō at 3:30 p.m. Justice Minister Koyama explained the contents of his report in detail and held important consultations on the attitude and policies that the government should take. He left at 4:20 p.m. After Prime Minister Saitō met with Finance Minister Takahashi today, his face appeared quite worried. The press corps interviewed the Prime Minister at this time, trying to ask questions, but his answers were not very clear, probably because he was afraid of affecting the political situation, so he denied everything. The situation of the Q&A is recorded below. The reporter asked, "Today, the Prime Minister has met with the Finance Minister. Did he try to persuade Finance Minister Takahashi, who has expressed his intention to resign, to stay?" The Prime Minister replied, "Absolutely not." The reporter asked, "Then will the cabinet decide to resign en masse after waiting for the Justice Minister's report?" The Prime Minister replied, "This matter cannot be decided now." The reporter asked, "Will a meeting of the three elders be convened before or after the regular cabinet meeting tomorrow?" The Prime Minister replied, "I haven't thought about it yet." Finance Minister Takahashi made the following remarks, "Today I met with the Prime Minister and did not discuss anything. If you want to find out the content of this meeting, please look at our faces and make your judgment. Regarding the Ministry of Finance case, Justice Minister Koyama will report in writing, so you can look at the document and wait for his explanation before deciding on an attitude. It is rumored that the Justice Minister's report will be on the 3rd of next month. It is not yet known when." (Japan United News dispatch, 28th)

(Tokyo) At 5:30 p.m. today, Chief Prosecutor Hayashi visited Justice Minister Koyama at his official residence and handed over the report on the Ministry of Finance case, which consisted of more than ten pages. Tonight, Justice Minister Koyama will read the report in detail. If the wording is not problematic, it can be reported at the cabinet meeting on the 29th. The political world is particularly nervous about the report, believing that there will be a political change soon. (Dentsu dispatch, 28th)

Shuntian Steamer Robbers Send Letter to Han Fuju Seeking Clemency, Sun Danlin Describes Escape 59

(Jinan) The robbers of the Shuntian steamer entrusted Sun Danlin to deliver a letter to Han Fuju. The envelope was addressed to Chairman Han Jun of the Shandong Provincial Government. The letter stated, "Respectfully presented to Chairman Han, I humbly submit that the Fishery Joint Association was established in Di and Zhan counties the year before last. Xu Ziping was publicly elected as chairman. Although he had improper conduct in the past, he has reformed himself after being elected as chairman. We were originally law-abiding citizens. To maintain local security and protect our homeland, we served in the Joint Association, bravely fighting the enemy and suppressing bandits, without the slightest concern for our lives. Brigade Commander Zhao Xinde of the 54th Brigade was stationed here. Although the Joint Association was established locally, it was under the command of the 58th Brigade. We absolutely obeyed orders without exception. If Your Excellency does not believe this, you can send someone to thoroughly investigate. We have devoted ourselves to protecting the local area and obeyed Brigade Commander Zhao. We can honestly say that we have done nothing wrong. Later, Xu Ziping was executed, and the Joint Association was completely disbanded. We were fortunate to escape capture. Although we escaped with our lives, we had no money to live on outside and no home to return to, so we were inevitably facing death. After thinking it over again and again, we had no other choice but to kidnap five Englishmen as temporary hostages. We earnestly implore Your Excellency to show us mercy and find a way for us to make a living. We will be forever grateful. We had no choice but to resort to this emergency measure. We humbly beg Your Excellency to be lenient and not punish us. We would be endlessly grateful. Respectfully presented to Chairman Han, humbly kneeling with grievances." It is noted that Xu Ziping was originally a bandit leader who was incorporated into the Joint Association before being executed. Han stated that if the bandits do not hand over the kidnapped Chinese, they will be severely suppressed. (28th dispatch)

(Tianjin) One of the civilian boats used by the Shuntian steamer robbers arrived at Dagu today. Chinese authorities detained the boat for questioning. If it is confirmed that they are robbers, they will be sent to court for trial. (28th Reuters dispatch)

(Qingdao) Sun Danlin arrived in Qingdao from Weihaiwei on the afternoon of the 26th. Mr. Sun told reporters that this robbery was the most unfortunate event he had encountered in his twelve years as an official, and it could be considered just retribution. However, he wondered why the others, who were innocent, had suffered such a great disaster. Moreover, he felt particularly saddened that he had escaped unharmed on the 26th. He then spoke of the harsh treatment by the bandits, stating that he argued that a scholar could be killed but not humiliated. Although the bandits were angry and pointed their guns at him, he was not afraid at all. Later, the bandit leader heard about this and ordered him to be brought over, treating him quite politely. Since he could speak English, he could help with the ransom negotiations. Therefore, he took the opportunity to explain the consequences, saying that this case was a major international incident that the government could not ignore. Furthermore, foreign warships were docked in Yantai and Weihai, and planes would come to bomb them. How would they deal with that? The next day, planes did indeed arrive, and the bandits panicked, realizing that he had not lied. The bandits first fired shots as a warning, which was essentially announcing to everyone that they were robbers. The planes received the signal and flew back and forth, dropping notices demanding the immediate release of the Englishmen, or they would be bombed. The bandits were terrified and first sent him and Nick out by boat, along with a letter asking the British to intercede with the government troops, urging them not to threaten them too much, and requesting that the Shandong provincial government incorporate them. His boat had not gone far when a second boat sped past, heading north, later found to be the boat sending Yamamoto to Tanggu. The third time, they sent out the remaining four Englishmen. The remaining eighteen Chinese were not wealthy. This incident, from all perspectives, was quite suspicious, possibly instigated by someone. He hoped that the authorities would resolve it quickly to prevent future trouble. Finally, he said that he had returned to Weihai to work with Mr. Li Hanping on mining matters, but unexpectedly encountered this incident. He was fortunate to have escaped. He spent three days in Weihai entertaining Chinese and foreign officials, delaying his trip. He arrived in Qingdao yesterday and will travel to Jinan tonight with Mayor Shen to meet with Han. He will then have to go to Beijing to present the details. (28th Central News Agency dispatch)

Japanese Military's "Who's Who": Predictions of Future Leaders 90

Next, let's discuss who will be the next Minister of the Navy. If Minister of the Army Hayashi stays in office, it will likely still be Osumi. But if Ugaki forms a cabinet, the situation might be different, because he was a brave warrior in the blockade of Lushun. When Lushun was blockaded for the third time, he commanded the Busan Maru, but unexpectedly, he survived due to engine trouble. At that time, he wrote a letter in blood to apologize to his superiors. This was the first step in his rise to prominence. Also, when he was young, he had a case of misconduct. Recently, he dismissed Major General Sakano over the Ugaki declaration issue. This shows a lack of internal organization. Although Sakano was too rash, Osumi may have gone too far. If he stays in office, he will inevitably relapse into his old ways, without a doubt.

Currently, there are eight admirals in the Navy: Kato, Yamamoto, Osumi, Kobayashi, Nomura, Nakamura, Suetsugu, and Nagano. Except for Osumi, none of them have experience as Minister of the Navy. If Osumi does not rise again, who among these seven can take on this role? In terms of controlling the entire Navy, Admiral Kato Kanji, the former commander-in-chief of the Navy, is the most suitable. After the death of Marshal Togo, he is the elder statesman of the Navy. Since the London Conference, he has been the chief leader of the hardliners. The civilian faction that opposed him has all fallen, such as Admirals Takedi, Taniguchi, Ambo, Yamanashi, Sakonji, and Terashima. Therefore, in a time of impending crisis, it would be appropriate to appoint him as Minister of the Navy. But whether he is a military administrator is a question. He was originally the commander of the fleet and chief of the naval general staff, so he has no experience in military administration. Therefore, he can only be Minister of the Navy in wartime. If Ugaki forms a cabinet, he will definitely not be able to take the stage. Next, Suetsugu Nobumasa, the commander of the Combined Fleet, who is of the same type as Kato, has also attracted attention, but unfortunately, he has no experience in military administration. He is just a naval officer on the bridge. Others, such as military councilor Yamamoto Ohfuku, is the nephew of Yamamoto Gonnohyoe. He was second in his class at the Naval Academy, with Tsukuto Jiro as the top student, and Osumi was third. Because he is the same type as Kato, he has no connection with the military administration department and has only served as commander of the garrison and fleet. He has not served as director or deputy director in the Ministry of the Navy. Therefore, the only ones who can become Minister of the Navy are Kobayashi and Nomura. Nomura is the most tolerant, knows the world situation well, and has deep insights. He is also a military administrator, but he is often seen as a civilian, so he is only suitable for Minister of the Navy in times of crisis. In addition, he lost his right eye when Shanghai celebrated the Emperor's birthday, which inevitably hinders his duties. Thus, among the admirals, the only one who can serve as Minister of the Navy is thought to be Kobayashi Teizo, because Kobayashi is neither a civilian nor a hardliner, but a neutral talent. His talent, experience, and reputation certainly qualify him to be Minister of the Navy. He has served as a senior aide in the Ministry of the Navy, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau, chief attendant at the Geneva Three-Power Conference, commander of the training fleet, Director of the Naval Construction Headquarters, Vice Minister, and Commander-in-Chief of the Combined Fleet. In terms of organizational ability, although he is slightly inferior to Kato, he is still a military administrator. If he does not come forward, then Nakamura Ryosan and Nagano Osami of the same lineage will surely be encouraged to rise.

The Peiping-Shenyang Through-Train Conference Held in Tianjin; Through-Train Service to Begin July 1 After Repeated Consultations Between China and Japan; Staff to Be Transferred from the Beining and South Manchuria Railways 91

A Tianjin dispatch states that the Peiping-Shenyang Through-Train Technical Conference has concluded, and through-train service will begin on July 1. Regarding the conference, it is reported that after Shibayama arrived in Tianjin by train on the morning of the 24th, he went to the Beining Railway Bureau Reception Office in the French Concession and met with Chen Xiangtao, manager of the China Travel Service, and his deputy, Zhou Shizhong, who had been invited by Yin Tong. They discussed the through-train issue. At noon that day, Yin Tong hosted a banquet at the reception office for Shibayama and Chen Xiangtao. At 11:00 PM, they gathered at the Beining Railway Bureau's official residence on Haihe Road to discuss the matter. The Beining Railway Bureau was represented by Yin Tong, Chen Qingwen (Chief of the Traffic Department), Xu Ji (Chief of the General Affairs Department), Wang Tianxuan (Chief of the Accounting Department), and Xue Fan (Chief of the Transportation Section). The China Travel Service was represented by Chen Xiangtao, Zhou Shizhong, Hu Shiyuan, and Cai Pingjiu. The Japanese side was represented by Shibayama and Suzuki, the director of the Tianjin branch of the Japan International Tourist Bureau. They studied the detailed rules of operation decided at the Dalian conference one by one, and decided that the Beining Railway, the China Travel Service, and the Japanese side would be responsible. Chen Xiangtao, representing the China Travel Service, then signed the contract. The meeting lasted a very long time, ending at 2:00 AM on the 25th. At 9:00 AM, Shibayama left Tianjin to return to Peiping. At noon, Yin Tong went to the Technical Committee building in the Beining Garden and invited Chen, Zhou, and others to hold further discussions to secretly discuss the procedures for implementing through-train service. At 1:00 PM, he hosted a banquet, inviting important officials from the railway bureau to attend. At around 2:00 PM, Yin convened a meeting in the auditorium of Ningyuan, gathering Deputy Director Xu Wenguo, Zheng Baozhao, and other important officials to instruct the heads of various departments on the matters that should be prepared. The meeting adjourned at around 6:00 PM. During the meeting, Nitta Ryo, the representative of the South Manchuria Railway Office in Tianjin, came to the railway bureau to discuss matters related to through-train service. Yin sent Yu, the deputy director of the General Affairs Department, to meet him and discuss the matter before he left. This is a general account of the discussions between China and Japan in Tianjin over the past two days regarding through-train service. As for the main organizers of the through-train service, according to information released by the Japan International Tourist Bureau, it will be named the "Oriental Travel Service." Both sides wanted to avoid using the terms "China," "Japan," or "International." The headquarters will likely be located in Shanhaiguan, with branches in Peiping, Tianjin, Shenyang, Jinzhou, and other places. There will be one president and one vice president. The president will be Chinese, internally designated as Chen Xiangtao. The company will have two departments: transportation and accounting, with two heads for each department, staffed by both Chinese and Japanese. All staff will be transferred from the South Manchuria Railway and the Beining Railway. On each train, ticket inspectors and train guards will still be responsible by the South Manchuria Railway and the Beining Railway in sections. The travel service will send people to monitor the train. All ticket fares and tickets will be handled by the travel service itself. The method is similar to that of the American sleeping car company operating sleeping cars on various railways in China and Europe. This meeting in Tianjin focused on completing the formalities. The date of through-train service was decided in Dalian, and through-train service will begin on July 1 without a doubt. (25th)

Discovery of Primitive Human Remains; Discovery of Artifacts from 100,000 to 200,000 Years Ago 93

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Liangguang Geological Survey Institute, as per usual practice, dispatches personnel to the field to carry out work during the autumn and winter seasons each year. In recent years, discoveries related to the geology and mineral resources of Liangguang have been made from time to time. This spring, the institute dispatched technician Xu Ruilin to investigate the mineral resources in the Yongning, Wuming, Longshan, Nama, Guode, and Longan areas of Guangxi. He has now completed his work and returned to the institute. According to the institute's announcement, the results obtained this time are excellent. The strata in various areas are generally quite complex. From the Cambrian period of the Paleozoic Era to the Quaternary period of the Cenozoic Era, traces of all epochs except the Ordovician strata were found. The brachiopods, corals, and foraminifera produced in the Permian and Carboniferous limestone, as well as the bivalves and dicotyledonous plant fossils in the Tertiary period, are particularly abundant and many are standardized fossils. The preservation of the specimens is also very perfect, which is rare elsewhere. In addition to the minerals discovered by predecessors, pyrite was discovered at Tianjing Ridge in Wuming this time, and several very valuable gold placer deposits were discovered at the eastern foot of Damingshan Mountain in the eastern district of Wuming. Therefore, the specimens collected this time are also particularly numerous. The specimens from Yongning, Wuming, and Longshan counties comprise seven large boxes, totaling several hundred pieces. Furthermore, mammalian skeletons and teeth from the Late Tertiary period were discovered within the territory of Wuming. According to the research of paleontology expert Dr. Zhang Xi'di, it was discovered that there were species of horses, deer, elephants, and pigs. Most notably, there was also a fragment of a primate tooth. At the same time, many stone tools such as stone axes, stone knives, and stone rings were discovered, which are considered to be relics of primitive humans from 100,000 to 200,000 years ago. This discovery has considerable value in anthropology and paleozoology. Dr. Zhang is currently very interested in this and, after detailed research, there may be further new discoveries. (March 20, Year 63)

Taiwan Residents' Disturbance in the Xiamen Bombing Case; The Reason is the Detective Search and Arrest of Japanese Taiwanese in Gambling Dens; Two Bombings Occurred Overnight, Taiwanese Held Weapons and Paraded 94

Xiamen Dispatch: The 20,000 Taiwanese residents in Xiamen, who have Japanese nationality,

are completely outside the scope of our country's laws and administration, and are governed by the Japanese consulate, thus forming a special phenomenon. Among them, in addition to legitimate merchants, there is a part that specializes in illegitimate occupations such as opium and gambling, also forming a special anomaly. Moreover, their operation of opium and gambling has long been an open secret. Their gambling dens and opium dens all hang signs with the name of a certain foreign firm as a signboard. The Xiamen Special Public Security Bureau's detective team has been strictly cracking down on gambling dens and opium dens in the city in recent weeks, and has cracked down on many locations. On the 20th, two gambling dens were searched in the city. One was the Qifa Foreign Firm in Dasheng Lane, which was a gambling den and opium den of Chen Kuozui, a Japanese national. Taiwanese and gamblers in the den fired seven shots to resist arrest. The detectives also returned fire. Eventually, they rushed into the den and arrested twenty-six gambling criminals, seizing various opium paraphernalia and taking them to the bureau. No one was injured. The other was the Shengmao Company in Huiling Palace, which was a gambling den of a British national, Wu. Thirty-five gambling criminals were arrested, and various opium paraphernalia were seized. Someone in the den also fired shots to demonstrate, but the detectives went upstairs and they dispersed. Afterward, the British gambling den did not cause any problems. Chen Kuozui of the Japanese Qifa Foreign Firm reported to the Japanese police department established by the Japanese consulate in Xiamen Chaiqiao. Chen is a committee member of the Taiwan Association's Xiamen Port District Security, and has an office in the gambling den, with the county signboard on the wall. Therefore, Chen reported to the Japanese consulate that the Taiwan Association's District Security Committee office was destroyed. The Japanese police department immediately sent Kato Sano to negotiate with the director of the Public Security Bureau, presenting two points: (1) The execution was not done in conjunction with the Japanese police; (2) The destruction was illegal. This case is currently under negotiation. The Taiwanese side believes that the detective team's search and arrest of the Qifa gambling den was a deliberate provocation. The detective team is also on alert, and the situation is tense. On the evening of the 21st, a liquor store named Siyi Chun (Siyi Chun Liquor

Store was established by Chen Qingmu, the fourth group leader, and the group's office is located on the third floor) downstairs of the fourth office of the detective team in Siming East Zhengkou, was suddenly attacked by four youths who threw a one-pound bomb into the store. Fortunately, it did not explode. For a time, the shops on Siming West Road, North Road, and Guankou were all closed, preventing bilateral conflicts. Fortunately, the detectives only guarded the team headquarters and did not go out, so no incident occurred. At two o'clock in the afternoon on the 22nd, more than a hundred people gathered in front of the Siyi Chun Liquor Store to demonstrate. The detectives still tried their best to avoid conflict. At about eight o'clock in the evening, a loud explosion suddenly occurred in front of the Southeast Inn on Siming North Road. The Southeast Inn was established by Taiwanese and is the main location of the special forces of the Taiwanese. A rickshaw puller, Shi Shui, fell to the ground on the spot, with both feet injured by the explosion. Another woman was slightly injured. After the explosion, the Taiwanese immediately took the excuse that someone had thrown a bomb at them, and divided more than a hundred people into five teams, each team of twenty to thirty people, each holding submachine guns, Browning pistols, and other firearms, patrolling and searching. When the citizens saw this, they were greatly alarmed. The night markets on Siming North and South Roads, Zhongshan Road, and Datong Road were all closed in succession, and there were no pedestrians on the roads. The detectives, on the other hand, when the Taiwanese patrolled with weapons, used dozens of people to guard Siyi Chun, the second and third floors, stairs, doors and windows, and the roof, all set up sandbags. The detectives from the Detective General Office and various team departments and groups also gathered in teams to be fully prepared, and no one went out, so no conflict occurred. At that time, Wang Guopan, director of the Public Security Bureau, went to a banquet hosted by Tsukamoto Takeshi, a Japanese official. Upon hearing the report, he immediately discussed with the Japanese consul and asked him to restrain the Taiwanese to prevent the matter from escalating. The Japanese consul immediately called Chen Changfu, chairman of the Taiwan Association, and instructed him to instruct the Taiwanese in each district to refrain from acting rashly. Wang Guopan also telegraphed the Public Security Bureau, ordering the security team and the entire police force to be dispatched for temporary martial law, and ordered Lian Liangshun, director of the Detective Office, to order the detectives not to go out, so as to avoid conflict. On one side, Xie Shaozeng, chief of the First Branch, and Sano, chief of the Japanese police department, went to the Southeast Inn to investigate and found out that the bomb was thrown on the pedestrian arcade pillar between the Southeast Inn and Shenghua Foreign Firm (both operated by Taiwanese from the same family). In addition to the two people injured by the explosion, the "Fa" character of the Shenghua Foreign Firm's signboard was blown through a hole, and a piece of glass was shattered. The explosive force was not strong, and it seemed to be homemade. At ten o'clock, the armed Taiwanese had all returned, but the whole night was serious, and it only eased on the morning of the 22nd. According to the injured rickshaw puller, Shi Shui, he was waiting for customers in the Siming Theater. Someone in front of the Southeast Inn called for a rickshaw. He pulled the rickshaw to the front and saw four people, two wearing Western-style clothes and two wearing short shirts and trousers, coming out of the Southeast, one of whom was holding something in his hand and threw it violently in the middle of the street. With a loud explosion, he felt a strange pain in both thighs and fell to the ground. He saw the four people still entering the Southeast and going upstairs, etc. Afterward, according to the rickshaw driver's statement, the Public Security Bureau believed that the Taiwanese threw it themselves and negotiated with the Japanese consul. However, according to the testimony of the shop staff of the Southeast Inn, the Japanese police department said that they saw a person in black shirt coming to the middle of the road and throwing it towards the Southeast, and it exploded on the pillar of the arcade. The shop staff started chasing him, and he escaped into the Nanhua Restaurant lane. It seemed that there were many people responding at the entrance of the alley before they stopped, etc. The Japanese consul promised to investigate the Public Security Bureau's negotiations. As a result of this conflict, which started with the search and arrest of Taiwanese gambling dens, the Japanese police chief Sato hosted a banquet on the evening of the 24th to appease the director of the Detective Office and the group leaders. As a result, the Japanese consul agreed to prohibit the Taiwanese from patrolling with guns in the future, but in the future, the Public Security Bureau must cooperate with the Japanese police in handling all cases involving Taiwanese. This matter was temporarily concluded. According to the regulations, before the September 18th Incident, our officials executed the search, arrest, and detention of Taiwanese, and the extradition was carried out after the case was settled. After the September 18th Incident until recently, the Taiwanese have been completely governed by the Japanese consulate. All cases involving Taiwanese must be searched and arrested in conjunction with the Japanese police and taken directly to the consulate by the Japanese police. (June 25)

Nine Women in Huian Formed an Alliance to Commit Suicide; Ages 13 to 19; Reasons for the Alliance and Motivation for Suicide 95

Xiamen Dispatch: Seven sisters surnamed Pan and two sisters surnamed Chen outside the North Gate of Huian County, Quanzhou Prefecture, formed an alliance to commit suicide, which has attracted great attention in southern Fujian society. The cause of this incident was that Pan Sheng, the daughter of Pan, married Shi Wenzhong in Shuangguibei last August. Shi later went astray and became a bandit. Pan repeatedly tried to correct him, but was often beaten. Since the woman was abused and unwilling to marry a bandit, she developed the idea of ​​being tired of the world. At the same time, Pan Ye, the daughter of Pan Tan, was betrothed by her parents to Chen Chunsheng as a daughter-in-law, but the Chen family already had an adopted daughter-in-law, and she felt that her future was not blessed. Also, Chen Huan, the sister of Chen Xuehua, was betrothed to the son of Wang Zhuo, but she disliked that her husband was weak. The three women then recruited nine sisters to form an alliance to commit suicide. On the 21st of this month, they gathered at their mothers' home, each changed into new clothes and pants of black gauze, wore wooden clogs, and at nine o'clock at night, they went to the Houzhai Pond outside the North Gate. The nine women took off their wooden clogs and lined them up by the pond, and then tied themselves together with ropes to form a string and threw themselves into the water together. When the family members found out the next morning, the nine women had all returned to the Heaven of Departing Sorrow, and the nine corpses were linked together inextricably. The names of the nine women are: Pan Songgu, 16 years old, daughter of Pan Yuanyuan, married He Qinglin in North Gate Street last August; Pan Sheng, 19 years old, married Shi Wenzhong; Pan Ye, 19 years old, daughter of Pan Tansheng, engaged to Chen Chunsheng's son, not yet married; Bo Guan, 15 years old, daughter of Pan Daofu, unmarried; Pan Qin, 17 years old, daughter of Pan Wutan, married to a Zhuang in the village; Pan Xi, 19 years old, sister of Pan Shenqiu, married Hu Lianfa last August, currently five months pregnant; daughter of Pan Zao (name unknown), 13 years old, unmarried; daughter of Chen Qingshui, 16 years old (name unknown), unmarried; Chen Huan, betrothed to Wang Zhuo's son, unmarried. Huian is a coastal county in Quanzhou Prefecture, and the women all have natural feet. All work, both agricultural and industrial, is done by women. They plow in the fields and carry burdens on the roads. Women from Huian are commonly seen as stone workers and dockworkers in Xiamen. Men, on the other hand, mostly stay at home, manage household affairs, and take care of children. Although women in Huian are economically independent and are the burden of the family, the authority of husbands in the family is still extremely heavy, and is even greater than in other places. Therefore, the status of women is still very low. In addition, except for Huibei, the entire county has a strange custom, that is, after a woman marries, she must still return to live in her mother's home. She only returns to her husband's home for a few days during the year-end holidays such as Lunar New Year's Eve and the Ghost Festival. The rest of the time she lives in her mother's home. Couples are separated, just like the Weaving Maiden in the sky. After women endure pain and loneliness, they often form alliances with sisters to comfort each other and complain to each other. The trend of alliance suicide has arisen from this. Among them, there are young girls who have not yet tasted life, who also join in suicide. According to the elders, dozens of years ago, those who formed an alliance to commit suicide were tied together and thrown into the water. In the past twenty years, this trend has gradually subsided. In recent years, it has almost disappeared. This time, nine people died together, which has not happened in fourteen or five years. Moreover, among these nine people, many were tired of the world because of marriage, but three of them were unmarried, and one of them was only 13 years old, so they completely joined the alliance emotionally. Their tying themselves into a formation was to show that they would not regret it until death, and to agree to die together. As soon as one person jumped into the water, they had to die together, and no one could change their mind halfway. Currently, the county party department has sent a letter to the county government regarding the occurrence of this case, urging them to pay attention. The letter said, "Respectfully, it has been reported that on the evening of the 21st, a case of women forming an alliance to commit suicide by throwing themselves into the water occurred in Beimendou, the city. As many as nine people died together, which is truly shocking. It has been found that in this county, except for Huibei, women only return to their husband's house for a few days during the year-end holidays such as Lunar New Year's Eve and the Ghost Festival. The rest of the time they are in their mothers' homes, resulting in the separation of husband and wife, alliances among sisters, and cases of suicide due to being tired of the world have emerged one after another. This kind of bad custom has been around for a long time. If it is not eradicated, the consequences will be dire. I hereby request that you investigate and thoroughly investigate the parents of the deceased in this case, and issue a notice to strictly prohibit it, so that couples can live together and share the happiness of the family, and the parents should strictly supervise them and not allow any unruly behavior, so as to respect human life and save the declining trend. (June 25)

Northwestern Inspection Notes; Special Correspondent Geng Ya; Mongolian Women Whose Power Exceeds Men's 96

On the morning of the eighth, because the camel drivers repeatedly asked to buy sheep to reward them, I and Mr. Zhu went to a Mongolian yurt. There was a dog as large as a small donkey, barking madly but not hurting people. The owner came out to see, and the barking stopped immediately. The owner was a female lama who did not understand the language. Mr. Zhu pointed to the sheep and calculated the price to show his intention to buy. She pretended not to understand, turned around and entered the yurt, and we returned empty-handed. The dog did not chase or bark. At two o'clock in the afternoon, we left Kushui Jingzi. The sandy land gradually decreased, and there was more clay. The dust from the camels was like setting off firecrackers. On the way, we met an old Mongolian man who said, "I have sheep I want to sell, the real price is eight yuan per head." We went to the pasture with him and saw his women lying naked on the ground. When guests arrived, they straightened their clothes to greet them. The women's heads were surrounded by tinkling ornaments, weighing more than a pound. The girls had no decorations, only two braids hanging down. Mr. Zhu gave the girl candy, and the mother and daughter each ate one. The rest were taken into the yurt, probably to be shared with others. We were about to lead the sheep we bought away on a donkey, when the woman said that it was not easy for a distant guest to come here, and returned one yuan as a birthday gift. Compared to the female lama we met in the morning, who had a cold face and an iron heart, it was unbelievable that they were of the same ethnic group. The woman chased after the camel team, traveling about ten miles back and forth, sweating like rain.

At eleven o'clock at night, we arrived at Baitu Jing and saw that the camel teams that had arrived earlier had occupied all the flat ground, so we had to find another Artemisia ground to pitch our tent and sleep. The journey that day was seventy li. The soil here is white like lime, and there are eight wells, several feet apart, with one sweet and seven bitter, which is very strange.

At eight o'clock in the morning on the ninth, the Suiyuan Huoyekuo Zhiju sent four armed soldiers and six plainclothes men to collect camel donations, two corners per load. Our team had seventy freight loads, and should have paid fourteen yuan. Mr. Zhou had served as the director of a public security bureau in a certain county, and mediated from the middle, so we settled for eight yuan. However, we carelessly issued donation tickets. Some of the other camel teams came forward, some paid silver, some issued tickets, and some did not issue tickets. Judging by the armbands worn by the donation collectors, one was "Suiyuan Provincial Government Inspection Office Huoye Branch," and the other was "Huoye Dizhiju." A certain camel team transporting wool to the east was secretly transporting opium, hidden in the camel saddles made of cloth, leather, and grass. The inspectors probed it with an iron bar and found it.

According to Mr. Shi Lianqing from Ningxia, the Huoye Dizhiju is located on the Taole Lake beach. The beach used to be the main stream of the Yellow River. During the Guangxu period, the river tilted westward, and silt accumulated to form the beach. According to legend, the two surnames, Tao and Le, grazed their animals there, hence the name. When the river shifted further west, the Dongyonghui Village and Wuduizi area in Pingluo County were completely washed away to the east of the river, and the residents moved there accordingly. Later, due to farming and grazing relations, a dispute arose between the Han and Mongolian over the beach. As a result of negotiations, a monument was erected as the boundary. The east of the monument was the pasture of the Otog Banner, and the west of the monument belonged to the Pingluo County of Ningxia. There were about a hundred households of residents, nine out of ten of whom were from Pingluo. Over the past ten years, only a few hundred hectares of land have been cultivated. The land is located between the Yellow River and the East Mountain, narrow and long from north to south for more than seventy li, and of varying width from east to west, averaging about three li. It is only a little over a hundred li away from Ningxia. Every year, Ningxia Province produces wool, hemp, licorice, wolfberries, hair vegetables, and other medicinal materials, most of which are transported out from this beach. Goods from Tianjin, Shanghai, Wuhan, and other places also enter Ningxia through this place. No matter what time, vehicles and horses are constantly passing through, especially in winter. It is truly an important transportation hub for the grassland. In October of the 18th year, the Ningxia Provincial Government drafted a governance plan, which was transferred to the Executive Yuan through the internal affairs department. Approval was given to establish the Dizhiju. The Suiyuan Provincial Government also advised the internal affairs department in November to establish the Huoye Dizhiju within the Otog Banner, and said that the Taole Beach was included in its administrative region, and the Ningxia Taole Beach Dizhiju should be abolished. The two sides repeatedly argued, and the result was that the Huoye Dizhiju was established. Currently, the people of Pingluo in Ningxia Province still believe that "Taole is the land silted up by Pingluo and should be governed by Ningxia Province. The boundary between the two provinces of Sui and Ning should be the Dongshan boundary monument, and the Yellow River, whose water flow is uncertain, cannot be relied upon" and other reasons, and continue to voice opposition. (It is noted that the Huoye Dizhiju is located in Taole, only a little over a hundred li away from Ningxia. The location recorded on the map is often erroneous.)

Baitu Jing is still more than a hundred li away from the Yellow River ferry. Someone sent a message saying, "The Tongchang ferry is calm and can be crossed." The messenger was dressed as a Mongolian man on horseback and was forty-two years old. He was originally from Shaanxi and had been working here since he was fifteen years old. The accumulation of more than twenty years of hard work and sweat has resulted in one hundred and fifty sheep and six horses, which can be considered a well-off family. However, he wants to marry a Mongolian woman, but is restricted by etiquette and has not been successful for a long time. Recently, Jia Lang, named "Buyingshu," under the jurisdiction of the Prince's Palace, consulted with "Sumuzhangge (official title) Baiyingdiuling (personal name)," gave him the Mongolian name "Daotouma," and pointed him to a widow, instructing him to marry her. However, the wealth demanded was very high. The woman's jewelry alone, two pairs of earrings and a string of beads, and the hanging temple peaks, cost more than thirty yuan, which is still considered to be of medium to low quality. If decorated with pearls (usually made of sheep bones dyed), the total price is even more limitless. Therefore, when calculating the property of Mongolian people, one should first look at the number of sheep and then observe the value of women's decorations, and then one can think more than half of it. When asked what the meaning of "Daotouma" is, he replied, "It means 'can stand'." As for the two names "Buyingshu" and "Baiyingdiuling," they mean "old rich man" and "wealthy for life."

Mongolian people's daily life: they get up at six o'clock in the morning, eat fried rice and butter tea, and then drive their livestock to drink water and graze in the wilderness. In the afternoon, at three or four o'clock, they drink tea and rice again, or they can bring dry food in the morning. Until six or seven o'clock, they drive the sheep into the pen in the afterglow of the setting sun, milk them, draw water, and have a busy dinner. Mutton porridge is eaten mostly at this time. In winter, when the snow is heavy, they stay at home and rarely go out, mostly only eating a full meal of mutton and drinking several bowls of thick tea melted from snow. The responsibilities of ordinary women are greater than those of men, so all the real power is also controlled by women. All things, from seeking water, sewing clothes, cooking food, herding sheep, and milking, are all done by women. Men mostly seek relatives and friends, travel far to worship Buddha, and gallop hundreds of miles, not returning for several days. Every year from July 14th to 16th, they travel thousands of miles, carrying abundant food, to gather at Zhaomiao Temple for the competition of jumping ghosts, horse racing, and wrestling. The prince also prepares silver dollars and tea bricks to reward the winners. This is truly a grand gathering for the Mongolian people who live scattered throughout the year to gather together for joy.

The main foods of the Mongolian people, besides mutton, rice, and tea, are butter. The method of making it is to squeeze the milk of cows and sheep every day, and put it in jars and bottles to ferment. If you steam fresh milk, a thin layer will form on the top, called milk skin, which is of good quality and high price. The remaining soup is used for tea drinking, and the concentrated substance that settles to the bottom is called Lao Danzi, also known as milk residue, which tastes sour and difficult to eat. At two o'clock in the afternoon, we set off from Baitu Jing. There was no water in the inn, so we borrowed four leather bags from the Mongolian people to transport it. We traveled seventy li and chose a place to camp, commonly known as "Guan Lingdu." On the way, we encountered a big wind, with tumbleweeds filling the sky and drifting sand covering the sun, a horrifying scene.

Songjiang; Establishment of the New Life Promotion Association 97

After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek announced the New Life Movement, various places followed suit. The county government of this county has repeatedly received provincial orders to expound the mysteries of the New Life Movement, and ordered local agencies to organize the New Life Movement Promotion Association to preside over its implementation. The county government complied and convened a meeting at the county government this afternoon (the 28th). Representatives from various agencies attended. Jin Liguan (Secretary Wu acting) presided over the meeting and decided to elect nine members to organize this association. The Anti-Smoking Committee Starts Work 98

This county was ordered to organize an Anti-Smoking Committee. The county magistrate, in accordance with the regulations, appointed Wang Zhewu, Yin Shisheng, and Zhang Shouzhi as members, in addition to himself and the director of the Public Security Bureau as ex officio members. However, Wang Zhewu, a member of the standing committee of the party department, sent a letter resigning. After the county magistrate urged him to come, he finally agreed. The committee was held yesterday and approved the candidates for secretary and deputy directors of each section, and decided to ask service personnel from all party, government, military, and academic circles to voluntarily report for a two-week abstinence period starting from the 15th of this month. If no one reports at the end of the period, the various agencies will issue a joint guarantee, and each agency will send a letter to each agency for inspection. It is reported that public officials are unwilling to report and have been flocking to the hospital to request smoking cessation, in order to break the addiction by the end of the period and not violate the provincial order.

Wuxi; Severe Drought Causes Rice Prices to Soar 99

The weather has been extremely hot in recent days, with the thermometer rising above 100 degrees, which has not been seen in sixty years. The weather has been dry for a long time without rain, the fields have cracked, the farmers cannot transplant rice seedlings, and the rice seedlings are gradually withering. In addition, the river water is shallow and dry, and the water-lifting machines and boats cannot enter the river banks, so it is difficult to lift water into the fields. A drought is about to occur. In recent days, the market prices of rice and wheat have soared. White rice has already risen from six yuan and nine corners per factory to nine yuan and five corners. Within a day or two, it may exceed the ten-yuan mark, and the people are extremely panicked. The price of wheat has also risen to more than five yuan per stone. According to the experience of fishermen, it will not rain until the beginning of autumn. Currently, most of the small wheel boats in the countryside cannot travel due to the dry water. The ferry crossings from this county to Qingyangbei and Jiuligang in the north of Nanzha have been cut off. There are more than eight hundred boats docked in the common area, and the food supplies of the boaters are cut off. They have been flocking to Qingyang Jihe Dai Nei to pawn goods. If this continues, the future is worrying. The villagers in the 17th district of this county have petitioned the authorities to dredge the Lüjiang Estuary. The Construction Bureau has sent personnel to the countryside to survey. The market price of watermelons was only about two yuan per load last year, but it has soared to eleven yuan per load this year.

County Chamber of Commerce Discusses Business Tax 100

The County Chamber of Commerce has received reports from various industries stating that the Business Tax Bureau's methods of assessment increase tax amounts, and that the annual investigations and disturbances are unbearable. Therefore, representatives from various industries were invited to solicit opinions and summarize the following measures: 1. Request the Business Tax Bureau to clearly announce to the Chamber of Commerce the business tax investigation figures for various industries since the establishment three years ago, as well as the actual receipts and increases/decreases for comparison. 2. If any industry experiences business downturns or shop closures, it should be reported to the Business Tax Bureau at any time, and the business tax payable should be deducted accordingly. The Business Tax Bureau must also reassess taxes based on the actual business conditions of each industry. 3. Each industry should inform its peers to promptly pay the business tax to the Business Tax Bureau according to the previously paid amount on a quarterly basis. If there is any obstruction to collection, the payable tax amount should be temporarily deposited into the Jiangsu Bank under a separate account for safekeeping and reported to the industry association, which will forward it to the Chamber of Commerce for reporting to the county government for record. 4. If the Business Tax Bureau uses provincial regulations as an excuse to investigate and disturb merchants again, causing business instability, the Chamber of Commerce and industry associations cannot be held responsible, and self-determination will be the only course of action.

Jiangyin: Man Sentenced to Death for Murdering His Husband 101

He Yunlin, a farmer from Daijia Village in Nanwai, died suddenly on the night of November 11, 1932, with an unclear cause of death. The county government detained his wife, He Chen, along with accomplices Kou Shilang, Dai Aliu, and Dai Zhan, for interrogation and detention. On March 20, 1931, the county court acquitted He Chen and the others. The case was sent to the High Court for review. Huang Baoquan and others from Nanwai filed an extraordinary appeal to seek justice for the deceased. The case was then remanded for retrial. Yesterday (26th), the county retrial concluded. He Chen was sentenced to death for premeditated murder, Kou Shilang was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for assisting in murder, Dai Zhan was sentenced to six years of imprisonment, and Dai Aliu was acquitted.

Zhenjiang: Buying Vegetables Leads to Fatal Conflict 102

Liu Jun, a 20-year-old from Suqian, residing at 57 Tangliu Lane in this port, had a verbal altercation with Yin Shunbao (also known as Da Guanzi), a vegetable buyer from No. 38 Genglou Lane, while buying vegetables the day before yesterday morning, resulting in a mutual fight. Liu Jun kicked Da Guanzi in the kidney, and Da Guanzi died at around 10 PM last night. Yin Shunxi, Da Guanzi's younger brother, upon seeing his brother's death, took Liu Jun to the Public Security Bureau, requesting justice and punishment for the murderer. The court prosecutor's office dispatched prosecutors to the scene yesterday (27th) at around 4 PM to conduct an autopsy. The deceased Yin Shunbao indeed had a wound on his lower abdomen. The body was ordered to be taken into custody pending investigation and handling.

Sailing boat workers from Twelve Weirs had repeatedly petitioned the Ministry of Finance in Beijing because motorized transport had encroached upon their livelihood. Subsequently, an order from the Ministry of Finance was received approving the conversion of 300 large and small motorized transport permits on the Hunan and Anhui coasts to sailing transport, and setting a two-week deadline for implementation. Now, four weeks have passed, and the transport has not yet been implemented. Therefore, on the 25th, representatives such as Duan Zhizhou and Yang Yunhan were sent again to the transport merchants on the four coasts to urge transport. After Duan and others arrived in Yangzhou, they held meetings at the offices of the four coasts for several days. As a result, the Hunan coast agreed to 121 permits (the weir representatives requested 189 permits), and the West Anhui coast agreed to 90 permits (the weir representatives requested 60 permits). Because no one has made contact on the Hubei coast, the representatives are still in Yangzhou, continuing discussions with the transport merchants.

Jiaxing: Filial Son Beats His Father to Death 109

In Shengdaozao, about three miles from Youchegang Town in the northern countryside of Jiaxing, there lived a farmer named Xu Sanmao, who was 64 years old. His son, Mao Wu, was already married. However, Mao Wu repeatedly beat his father. On the evening of the 25th of this month, Sanmao scolded his son for being lazy. Unexpectedly, Mao Wu used a long orange tree branch to beat his father violently. His father fled into the house. His daughter-in-law, Ms. So-and-so, helped her husband tie up his father with a rope and then beat him again. Finally, they abandoned the old father outside the door. After neighbors untied him, Sanmao spent the night outdoors and died the next day due to his serious injuries. Subsequently, the deceased's brother, Xu Dahe, bought a coffin and buried him, attempting to cover up the incident. However, the news spread, and the whole town knew about it. Therefore, the township head reported it to the public security station, which arrested the murderer Mao Wu. On the 28th, he was transferred to the Jiaxing local court for detention. Because the deceased had bloodstains on his forehead and bruises on his left and right ribs and waist, Wang Bangyan, the prosecutor of the Jiaxing local court prosecutor's office, went to the village on the 28th to conduct an autopsy.

Export Goods Tax Reduction Rates; No Additional Taxes Allowed; City Government Ordered to Notify 115

It has already been ordered and notified. In recent years, the export of bulk goods in our country has been mostly stagnant. The reason for this is due to the global economic panic, but high shipping costs and heavy taxes have been striking export goods. The Ministry of Finance's proposal to change tax rates this time aims to promote the development of domestic industries, expand overseas trade sales, and reduce the burden on merchants. Since the publication of the revised tax rates, the provincial and municipal governments should not add any additional taxes to the various goods with reduced export taxes in the amendment in the future, in order to comply with the central government's intention to promote industry and sympathize with merchants. In addition to separate orders, this order instructs compliance and directs subordinate units to comply accordingly. After the city government received the order, it has ordered its subordinate agencies to notify them all.

City Finance Bureau Schedules Rent Survey; Starting August 1st 118

The Municipal Finance Bureau has scheduled to start surveying rent prices on August 1st due to the increasing number of households and frequent changes in housing rental prices in the city. The announcement is as follows: The collection of housing donations has always been based on rent prices. Now, the number of households in the city is increasing, and housing rental prices are also changing frequently. In order for the bureau to calculate housing donations based on accurate rental prices and ensure that citizens bear a fair burden, we have specially formulated measures to investigate housing donations. Households with rental prices that do not match the donation amount will be re-estimated and an appropriate donation amount will be assessed for collection. If it is found that rental prices are deliberately concealed, in addition to recovering the concealed housing donations, a penalty of 20% of the donation amount to be supplemented will be imposed. However, the recovered amount will be limited to a maximum of one year's donation amount. It has been submitted to the city government for approval and implementation. The bureau has now scheduled to send personnel to start the investigation on August 1st. For all rented houses, if the rental price does not match the donation amount, the owner or tenant should report the correction before August 1st. If the house is self-built and self-occupied, and the calculated rental price does not match the current donation amount, the owner should also report the survey within the aforementioned deadline for reassessment. The donation amount for houses reported for correction and reassessment of rental price will be corrected and collected from this autumn, and no penalties will be imposed. Those who fail to report within the deadline will be dealt with according to the case after investigation without any leniency. When the bureau sends personnel to start the investigation, commercial and residential households in the city must submit the most recent rent receipt or lease or proof of the original estimated rental price to the investigators for review to facilitate the investigation and reporting. All investigators of the bureau will carry staff certificates with their photos attached to facilitate resident identification. If there are any impostors, citizens should turn them over to the nearest public security district office for legal action. If any investigators demand bribes, please report them truthfully, and they will be severely punished. In addition to sending letters to the Public Security Bureau to order its subordinate units to be informed, this announcement is made for general knowledge.

Current Fishing Season in Jiangsu and Zhejiang; Greatly Increased Fish Catches; Fishermen's Education Cannot be Delayed 120

Central News Agency reports that the current fishing season is about to end, so the situation in recent months is briefly described below. It is hoped that it will also be of interest to those concerned about the fishing industry.

Fishing Season Situation 121

The large yellow croaker and cuttlefish season usually starts after the beginning of summer. Fishing boats from the Taiwanese gang depart earlier, sailing north from the South Seas, fishing along various fishing ports such as Miaozi Lake, Qingbang, Huangxing, Changtu, Daishan, Maji, Dongsha Corner, and Huanglong. They will return to port after the Dragon Boat Festival. Fishing boats from Fenghua, Luomen, Dongmen, and Changtu, Zhejiang East gangs depart slightly later and must wait until the beginning of autumn to return to port. In addition, there are large teams of Ningbo fishing boats without any gang affiliation, temporarily gathering in areas such as Huanao, Bixia Mountain, Yemao Cave, and Dapan Mountain, specializing in catching cuttlefish and returning to port around early July.

Security Assured 122

At the beginning of this fishing season, the Fisheries Protection Office of the Ministry of Industry immediately sent various warships to patrol the fishing grounds in sections and temporarily transferred patrol boats to escort fishing gangs to the fishing grounds, providing extremely tight protection. Pirates were unable to steal, and the practice of pirates selling name cards also disappeared, reducing the burden on fishermen considerably. Also, in previous years' fishing seasons, disputes often arose among fishermen, especially between cage fishing and net fishing gangs catching cuttlefish, who would compete fiercely for fishing grounds, often resulting in hundreds of deaths and injuries. This year, the Fisheries Protection Office, seeing this, took preventive measures and sent a warship to be stationed permanently at the cuttlefish fishing grounds to suppress and maintain order. According to custom, the fishing grounds were divided, and each was not allowed to cross the border to fish. Therefore, this year, fishermen from various gangs were able to live peacefully and have not caused any trouble, making it the first peaceful year since the fishing season. What is unfortunate is that ignorant fishermen, due to the lack of proper entertainment venues, would go ashore to nearby towns to spend their time in improper businesses, which is a blemish on an otherwise perfect situation. Fishermen's education is an urgent and important task.

Increased Production 123

This year, due to the tireless efforts of the fisheries protection patrol boats, which were able to patrol the fishing grounds permanently, the sea was peaceful, and fishing boats from various gangs were able to boldly go to sea to fish, returning fully loaded, especially the Taiwanese gang, which could earn about 1,000 yuan per pair. The Fenghua, Daishan, Dongmen, and Ningbo gangs were next, followed by the Luomen gang. In general, they were all able to make a profit, unlike in previous years when there were uneven results and extreme differences in fortune. Also, this year, due to the increase in fish catches, ice-fresh boats from this port were extremely active in going to sea to buy fresh fish and made huge profits. Unfortunately, most of the coastal fishing factories have been seriously damaged due to years of losses and have weak purchasing power. Supply exceeds demand, and fishing boats have to sell their goods to the factories at low prices, and fishermen have to endure the pain. If fishing boats had such a abundant catch in previous years, the livelihood of the fishermen would have been prosperous. Therefore, the work of transporting fish catches to the interior for sale to stabilize fish prices is something that the government should pay attention to, which would benefit the national economy and people's livelihood considerably.

Families of Northeast Anti-Japanese Army Soldiers Receive Travel Expenses to Reunite in Xinjiang; Funds Distributed by Generals Ma, Su, Li, and Wang; Encouraging Voluntary Relocation to Xinjiang to Avoid Prolonged Separation 124

The various troops of former Northeast Anti-Japanese Army Generals Ma Zhanshan, Su Bingwen, Li Du, Wang Delin, and others, after being defeated and retreating into Russia and then being transferred to Xinjiang, numbered no less than tens of thousands of people. However, the families of various troops were stranded in Shanghai and other places, facing difficult lives. After repeated requests from Li Du and others, the central government allocated travel expenses to send the families of various troops to Xinjiang, so that families could be reunited, and they could concentrate on their duties and consolidate border defense, avoiding drifting in foreign lands without any support. It is learned that the central government sympathizes with the sacrifices and contributions of the soldiers of various troops in resisting the enemy and defending the country. The National Government has ordered the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Finance to quickly allocate funds and hand them over to Generals Ma, Su, Li, Wang, and others for distribution by name, so that various families can voluntarily relocate to Xinjiang to find their family members and avoid prolonged separation.

Ministry of Industry Sends Personnel to Shanghai to Investigate Machinery Supply and Demand; Situ Xi to Arrive in Shanghai Soon 125

Since the factory is in its initial stage, it is necessary to first understand the actual machinery needs of various factories in the country and the manufacturing situation of existing machinery factories in order to make future manufacturing plans, so that supply and demand can correspond and duplication can be avoided.
